# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
the signed area is the area made by the curve of the function as calculated with infinitely small rectangles
with height the instantaneous rate of change of such function ^g9MH0fpT

convert to polar form
set equality with (r(cosa+isina))^n
compare the two moduluses
set angles equality as na=2mpi
find a
state a for m = 1...n
combine ^ri2aGd54

the equality for the angle should be na=t+2mpi
where a is the base angle and t is the angle
from the conversion of the number to polar
form ^GYRUG6NC

%%
